| <span data-ttu-id="6fead-454">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6fead-454">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="6fead-455">Valor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6fead-455">Value</span></span> |

## <a name="windows-server-2008-r2"></a><span data-ttu-id="6fead-1159">Windows Server 2008 R2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6fead-1159">Windows Server 2008 R2</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="6fead-1160">Atributos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6fead-1160">Attributes</span></span>](#windows-server-2008-r2-attributes)
